The issue might be: 1. Not enough parallelism (only 256 blocks) 2. Strided memory access pattern 3. Per-block work too small to hide latency Let me try increasing num_splits further. With PAGES_PER_SPLIT=8, num_splits=8, total_blocks=512. Per block: 8 iterations, 64KB memory. Or with PAGES_PER_SPLIT=4, num_splits=16, total_blocks=1024. Per block: 4 iterations, 32KB memory. Let me try different values. Actually wait, I realize one thing. For shape 0, with PAGES_PER_SPLIT=16 and 4 splits, each block does 16 page iterations. The total tokens is 64*16 = 1024 = L. Good. The acc state is (G, D) = (4, 128) = 512 elements fp32 = 2KB. The Q is (4, 128) bf16 = 1KB. K per page is 4KB. V per page is 4KB. If I do pipelining with num_stages=2, we hold 2 K and 2 V in flight = 16KB. Plus scores, p_block, etc. Total ~20KB. Fine. The actual issue might be that the SM has many blocks (256) but only 82 SMs. So 3 blocks per SM. Each SM has multiple blocks to schedule. Each SM has 4 schedulers, each can issue 1 instruction per cycle. With 3 blocks per SM, the SM scheduler can pick from 3 blocks. If a block is stalled on memory, the scheduler picks another. For memory-bound kernels, the goal is to keep many memory requests in flight. Each SM can have ~256 in-flight loads (theoretical). With 3 blocks per SM, the per-block in-flight requests are limited by the per-block work. For a block with 16 iterations, we have 16 K loads and 16 V loads. With num_stages=2, we have 2 K and 2 V in flight = 4 in-flight loads per block. Per SM, 3 blocks * 4 = 12 in-flight loads. That's low. For more in-flight loads, we need more blocks per SM (more parallelism) or more stages (more pipelining). num_stages=4 would give 8 in-flight per block, 24 per SM. But might exceed register budget. Actually let me reconsider. Each block has 16 iterations, and num_stages=2 means 2 iterations in flight. Each iteration has 1 K load and 1 V load. So 4 in-flight loads per block. If I do num_stages=4, we'd have 4 iterations in flight, 8 in-flight loads per block. 3 blocks * 8 = 24 per SM. Better. But num_stages=4 uses more registers. Per iteration: K (4KB) + V (4KB) + scores (256B) + p_block (256B) + Q (1KB) + acc (2KB) = ~12KB. With 4 stages: 48KB. Per warp (32 threads): 48KB/32 = 1.5KB = 384 fp32 registers. Too many. So num_stages=2 is the max for shape 0. We're already at that. The alternative: more blocks (smaller PAGES_PER_SPLIT). With PAGES_PER_SPLIT=8: 2x more blocks, 2x more in-flight per SM. Let me try. Actually wait, I have an idea. What if I use a much larger block dim? Like G=8 instead of 4? For G=4, each block has 4 query heads. For G=8, 8 query heads. The compute is 2x but the memory is the same. The advantage: more in-flight compute to overlap with memory. The disadvantage: 2x compute (but we're memory-bound so it doesn't matter). import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math

# Monkeypatch the heuristic to use a fixed pps
def _fixed_pps(batch, num_kv_heads, seq_len, page_size, fixed_pps):
    num_pages = (seq_len + page_size - 1) // page_size
    if num_pages == 0:
        return 1, 1
    pps = fixed_pps
    num_splits = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps
    return pps, num_splits

def time_shape(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, fixed_pps, n_warmup=5, n_iter=20):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    # Patch the split params
    pps, ns = _fixed_pps(B, Hkv, L, P, fixed_pps)
    class PatchedModel(solution.Model):
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw):
            super().__init__(*a, **kw)
            self.pages_per_split = pps
            self.num_splits = ns
    sol = PatchedModel(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    for _ in range(n_warmup):
        sol(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        sol(*inputs)
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

shapes = [
    ('shape0', 8, 32, 8, 128, 1024, 16),
    ('shape1', 32, 32, 8, 128, 2048, 16),
    ('shape2', 4, 64, 8, 128, 4096, 16),
    ('shape3', 16, 32, 8, 128, 1535, 16),
    ('shape4', 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16),
]

# Get reference output for correctness
ref_outs = []
for sh in shapes:
    B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    ref = reference.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    ref_outs.append(ref(*inputs))

# Try different PAGES_PER_SPLIT
for pps in [4, 8, 16, 32, 64, 128]:
    gmean_log = 0
    count = 0
    times_per_shape = []
    for sh in shapes:
        B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
        median = time_shape(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps)
        bytes_moved = 2 * B * L * Hkv * D * 2 + B * H * D * 2 * 2
        gbps = bytes_moved / median / 1000
        # Score
        peak_gbps = 936.0
        frac = gbps / peak_gbps
        times_per_shape.append(median)
        import math
        gmean_log += math.log(max(frac, 1e-9))
        count += 1
    gmean = math.exp(gmean_log / count)
    print(f'PPS={pps:3d} ' + ' '.join(f'{t*1000:5.0f}us' for t in times_per_shape) + f'  gmean={gmean:.4f}')

import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import triton
import triton.language as tl
import math

# Make a copy of the kernel and try different num_warps
import math as _math
import torch as _torch
import torch.nn as _nn

# Try just changing the num_warps by wrapping the launch
@triton.jit
def _paged_decode_split_kernel(
    Q_ptr, KV_ptr, BT_ptr, SL_ptr,
    M_ptr, L_ptr, ACC_ptr,
    stride_qb, stride_qh,
    stride_kvp, stride_kvt, stride_kvh,
    stride_btb,
    stride_mb, stride_mh, stride_ms,
    stride_lb, stride_lh, stride_ls,
    stride_accb, stride_acch, stride_accs,
    SCALE: tl.constexpr,
    G: tl.constexpr,
    D: tl.constexpr,
    P: tl.constexpr,
    PAGES_PER_SPLIT: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_b = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_hkv = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_split = tl.program_id(2)
    seq_len = tl.load(SL_ptr + pid_b)
    num_pages = tl.cdiv(seq_len, P)
    page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT
    page_end = tl.minimum(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages)
    head_offs = pid_hkv * G + tl.arange(0, G)
    d_offs = tl.arange(0, D)
    q_ptrs = (Q_ptr + pid_b * stride_qb
              + head_offs[:, None] * stride_qh
              + d_offs[None, :])
    q = tl.load(q_ptrs)
    m_i = tl.full((G,), -float('inf'), dtype=tl.float32)
    l_i = tl.zeros((G,), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc = tl.zeros((G, D), dtype=tl.float32)
    t_offs = tl.arange(0, P)
    for p_idx in tl.range(page_start, page_end, num_stages=2):
        page_id = tl.load(BT_ptr + pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx).to(tl.int64)
        page_token_start = p_idx * P
        token_mask = (page_token_start + t_offs) < seq_len
        base = (KV_ptr + page_id * stride_kvp
                + t_offs[:, None] * stride_kvt
                + pid_hkv * stride_kvh)
        k_ptrs = base + d_offs[None, :]
        v_ptrs = base + (D + d_offs[None, :])
        k = tl.load(k_ptrs, mask=token_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        v = tl.load(v_ptrs, mask=token_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        scores = tl.dot(q, tl.trans(k)) * SCALE
        scores = tl.where(token_mask[None, :], scores, -float('inf'))
        m_new = tl.maximum(m_i, tl.max(scores, axis=1))
        alpha = tl.exp(m_i - m_new)
        p_block = tl.exp(scores - m_new[:, None])
        l_i = l_i * alpha + tl.sum(p_block, axis=1)
        acc = acc * alpha[:, None] + tl.dot(p_block.to(v.dtype), v)
        m_i = m_new
    g_offs = tl.arange(0, G)
    m_ptrs = (M_ptr + pid_b * stride_mb + pid_hkv * stride_mh
              + pid_split * stride_ms + g_offs)
    l_ptrs = (L_ptr + pid_b * stride_lb + pid_hkv * stride_lh
              + pid_split * stride_ls + g_offs)
    tl.store(m_ptrs, m_i)
    tl.store(l_ptrs, l_i)
    acc_ptrs = (ACC_ptr + pid_b * stride_accb + pid_hkv * stride_acch
                + pid_split * stride_accs
                + g_offs[:, None] * D + d_offs[None, :])
    tl.store(acc_ptrs, acc)

    mp = _torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=_torch.float32, device='cu

    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    
    # Build a wrapped model that injects num_warps
    class PatchedModel(solution.Model):
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw):
            super().__init__(*a, **kw)
            self.pages_per_split = pps
            self.num_splits = (self.seq_len // self.page_size + pps - 1) // pps
            self._n_warps = n_warps
        
        def forward(self, q, kvc, bt, sl):
            # Call the underlying function with num_warps injection
            import math as m
            B, H, D = q.shape
            Hkv = self.num_kv_heads
            G = H // Hkv
            P = self.page_size
            scale = 1.0 / m.sqrt(D)
            num_splits = self.num_splits
            pps = self.pages_per_split
            mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=q.dtype, device=q.device)
            grid_split = (B, Hkv, num_splits)
            solution._paged_decode_split_kernel[grid_split](
                q, kvc, bt, sl, mp, lp, ap,
                q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
                kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
                bt.stride(0),
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                SCALE=scale,
                G=G, D=D, P=P, PAGES_PER_SPLIT=pps,
                num_warps=self._n_warps,
            )
            grid_reduce = (B, Hkv)
            solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[grid_reduce](
                mp, lp, ap, out,
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
                G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=num_splits,
            )
            return out
    
    sol = PatchedModel(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    for _ in range(n_warmup):
        sol(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        sol(*inputs)
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

    ('shape2', 4, 64, 8, 128, 4096, 16),
    ('shape3', 16, 32, 8, 128, 1535, 16),
    ('shape4', 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16),
]

for nw in [1, 2, 4, 8]:

    count = 0
    times = []
    for sh in shapes:
        B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
        pps = 8
        t = time_shape_full(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, nw, pps)
        bytes_moved = 2 * B * L * Hkv * D * 2 + B * H * D * 2 * 2
        gbps = bytes_moved / t / 1000
        frac = gbps / 936.0
        log_sum += math.log(max(frac, 1e-9))
        count += 1
        times.append(t

import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math
import triton
import triton.language as tl


# Modified kernel with alignment hints
@triton.jit
def _paged_decode_split_kernel_v2(
    Q_ptr, KV_ptr, BT_ptr, SL_ptr,
    M_ptr, L_ptr, ACC_ptr,
    stride_qb, stride_qh,
    stride_kvp, stride_kvt, stride_kvh,
    stride_btb,
    stride_mb, stride_mh, stride_ms,
    stride_lb, stride_lh, stride_ls,
    stride_accb, stride_acch, stride_accs,
    SCALE: tl.constexpr,
    G: tl.constexpr,
    D: tl.constexpr,
    P: tl.constexpr,
    PAGES_PER_SPLIT: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_b = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_hkv = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_split = tl.program_id(2)
    seq_len = tl.load(SL_ptr + pid_b)
    num_pages = tl.cdiv(seq_len, P)
    page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT
    page_end = tl.minimum(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages)
    head_offs = pid_hkv * G + tl.arange(0, G)
    d_offs = tl.arange(0, D)
    d_offs = tl.max_contiguous(tl.multiple_of(d_offs, 8), 8)  # hint 8-way contiguous
    q_ptrs = (Q_ptr + pid_b * stride_qb
              + head_offs[:, None] * stride_qh
              + d_offs[None, :])
    q = tl.load(q_ptrs)
    m_i = tl.full((G,), -float('inf'), dtype=tl.float32)
    l_i = tl.zeros((G,), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc = tl.zeros((G, D), dtype=tl.float32)
    t_offs = tl.arange(0, P)
    for p_idx in tl.range(page_start, page_end, num_stages=2):
        page_id = tl.load(BT_ptr + pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx).to(tl.int64)
        page_token_start = p_idx * P
        token_mask = (page_token_start + t_offs) < seq_len
        base = (KV_ptr + page_id * stride_kvp
                + t_offs[:, None] * stride_kvt
                + pid_hkv * stride_kvh)
        k_ptrs = base + d_offs[None, :]
        v_ptrs = base + (D + d_offs[None, :])
        k = tl.load(k_ptrs, mask=token_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        v = tl.load(v_ptrs, mask=token_mask[:, None], other=0.0)
        scores = tl.dot(q, tl.trans(k)) * SCALE
        scores = tl.where(token_mask[None, :], scores, -float('inf'))
        m_new = tl.maximum(m_i, tl.max(scores, axis=1))
        alpha = tl.exp(m_i - m_new)
        p_block = tl.exp(scores - m_new[:, None])
        l_i = l_i * alpha + tl.sum(p_block, axis=1)
        acc = acc * alpha[:, None] + tl.dot(p_block.to(v.dtype), v)
        m_i = m_new
    g_offs = tl.arange(0, G)
    m_ptrs = (M_ptr + pid_b * stride_mb + pid_hkv * stride_mh
              + pid_split * stride_ms + g_offs)
    l_ptrs = (L_ptr + pid_b * stride_lb + pid_hkv * stride_lh
              + pid_split * stride_ls + g_offs)
    tl.store(m_ptrs, m_i)
    tl.store(l_ptrs, l_i)
    acc_ptrs = (ACC_ptr + pid_b * stride_accb + pid_hkv * stride_acch
                + pid_split * stride_accs
                + g_offs[:, None] * D + d_offs[None, :])
    tl.store(acc_ptrs, acc)


def time_shape_v2(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, n_warmup=5, n_iter=30):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    pps = 8
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    num_splits = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps
    q = torch.randn(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda') * 0.1
    kvc = torch.randn(64*16, P, Hkv, 2*D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda') * 0.1
    bt = torch.zeros(B, num_pages, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
    sl = torch.full((B,), L, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
    out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')

_l2_scratch = None
def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(128 * 1024 * 1024 // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()

@triton.jit
def _paged_decode_split_kernel_v2(
    Q_ptr, KV_ptr, BT_ptr, SL_ptr,

+    The heuristic balances two regimes:
+      - Small B*Hkv: increase parallelism with smaller PAGES_PER_SPLIT.
+      - Large B*Hkv*L: prefer larger PAGES_PER_SPLIT (more in-flight

For (P, 2D), the data is in row-major: P rows, each with 2D elements. The K is the first D, V is the last D. For (P, D) K and (P, D) V separately, the data is also in row-major: P rows, each with D elements for K, and P rows, each with D elements for V. The combined load reads 2D contiguous elements per row. The separate loads read D + D contiguous elements per row, but with a gap of (Hkv-1)*2D between K rows of different heads. Wait, the gap is between K rows of different (t, hkv), not within a (t, hkv). For the same (t, hkv), K and V are adjacent. So: - Combined: 2D contiguous elements per (t, hkv) row, with 2D*hkv + (P-1-t)*2D*hkv + ... gap between rows - Separate: D contiguous elements for K, then D for V (total 2D per row), with same gap The two should be equivalent in terms of total bytes. The combined load just does it in one operation. Hmm, so why is the combined load slower? Maybe the issue is the reshape and split operations in the kernel. But the load is strided (each column is 4096 bytes apart). This is worse for memory access. Hmm, trade-off. Let me try. Actually, for tl.dot to use tensor cores efficiently, the inputs should be in a specific layout. The natural layout is row-major. (P, D) and (D, P) are both row-major, just transposed. Triton's tl.dot can handle both. The question is which is more efficient given our memory layout. OK let me just try. Actually, let me also think about: maybe the issue is that my K trans is slow. Same result but different access pattern. Or: compute scores[h, t] = sum_d q[h, d] * k[t, d]. This is a dot product for each (h, t). 4 * 16 = 64 dot products, each of length D=128. In Triton, this is `tl.sum(q[h, :] * k[t, :], axis=...)`. But this is not a matrix multiply, and might be slow. OK let me just try the CUDA approach. I'll write a simple CUDA kernel. Actually, you know what, let me also try: vectorize the loads. For the K load, each row is 128 bf16 = 256 bytes. With 32 threads in a warp, each thread loads 8 bytes = 4 bf16. The 32 threads load 32*4 = 128 bf16 = 256 bytes. This is 2 cache lines (128 bytes each). If we use 16-byte loads (8 bf16 per thread), the 32 threads load 32*8 = 256 bf16 = 512 bytes. This is 4 cache lines. The 16-byte load is one instruction (LDG.E.128 on Ampere). The 8-byte load is also one instruction (LDG.E.64). Same number of instructions, more data per warp. For the K row of 128 bf16 (256 bytes), 8-byte loads need 2 LDG per warp. 16-byte loads need 1 LDG per warp. So 16-byte loads are more efficient per warp. Triton should do this automatically if the data is aligned. In Triton, the load size is determined by the compiler based on the data layout. We can hint with `tl.max_contiguous`. The current kernel handles G query heads per block. What if we handle more, say G_max where G_max is the next power of 2 >= G? For G=4, G_max=8. For G=8, G_max=8. For G_max=8 with G_real=4: - We load 8 query heads, but only 4 are real - The other 4 are zero - The compute handles 8 heads, but only 4 contribute to the output - The output write needs to be careful This effectively doubles the compute but uses tensor cores more efficiently. For memory-bound kernels, the extra compute is free (hidden by memory). Let me try G_max=8 for G_real=4 shapes. For G_real=8 (shape 2), G_max=8 (no padding needed). 93	
94	        scores = tl.dot(q, tl.trans(k)) * SCALE  # (G, P), fp32
95	        scores = tl.where(token_mask[None, :], scores, -float('inf'))
96	
97	        m_new = tl.maximum(m_i, tl.max(scores, axis=1))      # (G,)
98	        alpha = tl.exp(m_i - m_new)                          # (G,)
99	        p_block = tl.exp(scores - m_new[:, None])            # (G, P)
100	        l_i = l_i * alpha + tl.sum(p_block, axis=1)          # (G,)
101	        acc = acc * alpha[:, None] + tl.dot(p_block.to(v.dtype), v)  # (G, D)
102	        m_i = m_new
103	
104	    # Write partials
105	    g_offs = tl.arange(0, G)

1	"""Paged attention decode kernel (Triton) for SM86 (RTX 3090).
2	
3	Two-stage FlashDecoding approach for high SM utilization on small batches:
4	  Stage 1 (split): each (batch, kv_head, split) program processes a chunk of
5	                   pages for that kv_head and writes partial (m, l, acc).
6	  Stage 2 (reduce): combine splits per (batch, kv_head) into the final output.
7

For Q @ K^T: - Q is (G, D) = (4, 128) - K^T is (D, P) = (128, 16) - Result is (G, P) = (4, 16) In Triton, `tl.dot(q, tl.trans(k))` does this. The trans is in registers/shared memory. Alternative: use `tl.dot(k, q, trans_a=True)` to get (P, G) = (16, 4). Then transpose. Hmm same. Alternative: use the natural layout. K is (P, D). Q is (G, D). We want Q @ K^T = (G, P). The natural matmul A @ B with A=(G, D) and B=(D, P) requires B^T. So we either transpose B or do A @ B^T explicitly. Actually, tl.dot has an `acc` parameter for accumulation. Maybe I can use that. Actually, I want to try one more Triton variant. What if I use `tl.dot(q, k_t)` where k_t is the (D, P) view of K, but load it with the right strides? For K stored as (P, D) row-major, to view as (D, P), we need to read K[p, d] as K_t[d, p]. The natural order is (p, d) but we want (d, p). If we load with strides (stride_p=1, stride_d=D), we get the natural (P, D) order. To get (D, P), we'd swap the strides. In Triton, we can use `tl.make_block_ptr` or just provide strides: ```python k_t_ptrs = KV_ptr + page_id*stride_kvp + t_offs[None, :]*stride_kvt + pid_hkv*stride_kvh + d_offs[:, None] # k_t_ptrs[d, t] = KV_ptr + ... + t * stride_kvt + d # = K[t, d] (the natural access) # So loading gives us K in (D, P) layout k_t = tl.load(k_t_ptrs, mask=token_mask[None, :], other=0.0) # (D, P) scores = tl.dot(q, k_t) * SCALE # (G, P) - no transpose needed! ``` The K is now (D, P) in our hands, no transpose needed for the matmul. The load has strides (stride_kvt, 1), which is the strided access (d_offs[:, None] has stride 1, t_offs[None, :] has stride stride_kvt = 2048). The load is strided: each row is 16 bf16 contiguous (one token), and there are 128 rows. Same total data as before. But the access pattern is different. In Triton, the compiler will vectorize the load if the contiguous dimension is 16 bf16. With 32 threads in a warp and 16 elements per row, we can do 1 LDG.32 (32 bytes) per thread, or 2 LDG.16 (16 bytes each). Hmm, the strided load might be slower than the contiguous one (in the (P, D) version). Let me think. For (P, D) = (16, 128) load: 32 threads load 4 bf16 each = 128 bf16 = 256 bytes. The 16 elements per thread, 8 in the D direction (contiguous) and 1 in the P direction (strided). So 8 contiguous bf16 per "vector". For (D, P) = (128, 16) load: 32 threads load 4 bf16 each = 128 bf16 = 256 bytes. The 16 elements per thread, 1 in the D direction (1 bf16 contiguous, then stride) and 16 in the P direction (16 contiguous). Hmm. Wait, for the (D, P) layout, the strided dimension is D. For one t (column), the D elements are at stride stride_kvt = 2048 elements apart in memory. So contiguous in memory is P (16 elements per row). For the load (D, P) = (128, 16): - 32 threads load 4 elements each - 4 * 32 = 128 elements per instruction - 16 elements per column (P dimension) - 8 columns per instruction (D direction) - 16 instructions per warp (128/8) For each instruction, the 32 threads load 128 contiguous elements (across columns). These 128 elements are 16 per column * 8 columns. Within a column, 16 contiguous bf16. Across columns, 4096-byte stride. So the 32 threads load 32 elements, each at a different (d, t) but in a "strided" pattern within the 8 columns. Hmm, this is getting confusing. Let me just try it. Actually, I think the (D, P) layout might be worse for the load because the contiguous dimension is smaller (16 vs 128). Let me think. Within a row, 16 contiguous. Across rows, 4096-byte stride. - 16 instructions per warp to load 2048 elements So both have 16 instructions per warp. The difference is the data layout. For (P, D) layout: 4 elements per thread, contiguous in D. For (D, P) layout: 4 elements per thread, contiguous in P. The contiguous dimension is smaller in (D, P) (16 vs 128). // Paged attention decode split kernel (CUDA C++)
// One block per (batch, kv_head, split). Each block iterates over its pages,
// accumulating online softmax and writing partial m, l, acc.
//
// Layout assumptions:
//   Q:       (B, H, D)                                bf16
//   KV:      (num_blocks, P, Hkv, 2*D)                bf16, [K | V] packed
//   BT:      (B, max_pages)                           int32
//   SL:      (B,)                                     int32
//   M, L:    (B, Hkv, NUM_SPLITS, G)                  fp32
//   ACC:     (B, Hkv, NUM_SPLITS, G, D)               fp32

#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <cuda_fp16.h>

#include <torch/extension.h>

// Vectorized load helper: 4 bf16 = 8 bytes = uint64_t
typedef uint64_t bf16x4;
typedef struct __align__(16) bf16x8 { uint64_t a, b; } bf16x8;

template <int G, int D, int P, int PAGES_PER_SPLIT, int THREADS>
__global__ __launch_bounds__(THREADS) void paged_decode_split_kernel(
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Q,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ KV,
    const int* __restrict__ BT,
    const int* __restrict__ SL,
    float* __restrict__ M_partial,
    float* __restrict__ L_partial,
    float* __restrict__ ACC_partial,
    int stride_qb, int stride_qh,
    int stride_kvp, int stride_kvt, int stride_kvh,
    int stride_btb,
    int stride_mb, int stride_mh, int stride_ms,
    int stride_lb, int stride_lh, int stride_ls,
    int stride_accb, int stride_acch, int stride_accs,
    float scale
) {
    int pid_b = blockIdx.x;
    int pid_hkv = blockIdx.y;
    int pid_split = blockIdx.z;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;

    int seq_len = SL[pid_b];
    int num_pages = (seq_len + P - 1) / P;
    int page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT;
    int page_end = min(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages);

    // Q tile: (G, D) = (4, 128) = 512 bf16 = 1KB. With 128 threads, 4 elements/thread.
    // Use shared memory for Q.
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 q_smem[G * D];
    // Acc tile: (G, D) fp32 = 4*128*4 = 2KB.
    __shared__ float acc_smem[G * D];

    // Per-thread accumulators
    // Each thread handles a row of acc (G/D per thread? No, we want each thread to handle a column or a part)
    // For G=4, D=128: we can have 4 threads per row of D, with each thread handling D/4=32 elements
    // Or 1 thread per row, with each thread handling all D=128 elements

    // Simple: each thread handles a (g, d_chunk) for acc. 
    // For G=4, D=128, with 128 threads: 1 thread per (g, d) element
    // Per thread: 1 acc element, needs to compute scores[g, p] and accumulate

    // Load Q
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) {
        int g = i / D;
        int d = i % D;
        int q_off = pid_b * stride_qb + (pid_hkv * G + g) * stride_qh + d;
        q_smem[i] = Q[q_off];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Initialize acc in shared memory
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) {
        acc_smem[i] = 0.0f;
    }
    // Per-thread max and sum
    __shared__ float m_smem[G];
    __shared__ float l_smem[G];
    if (tid < G) {
        m_smem[tid] = -INFINITY;
        l_smem[tid] = 0.0f;
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Iterate over pages
    for (int p_idx = page_start; p_idx < page_end; p_idx++) {
        int page_id = BT[pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx];
        int page_token_start = p_idx * P;

        // Load K and V: K is (P, D), V is (P, D)
        // Per page: P*D*2 bytes for K + same for V = 4*P*D bytes
        // For P=16, D=128: 8KB per page
        // With 128 threads: 8KB / 128 / 2 = 32 bytes per thread = 16 bf16 per thread
        // We load 16 bf16 per thread (1 bf16x8 + 1 bf16x8)

        __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 k_smem[P * D];
        __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 v_smem[P * D];

        // Vectorized load: 8 bf16 = 16 bytes per thread
        // P*D*2 bytes / 16 = P*D/8 elements per thread
        // For P=16, D=128: 16*128*2/16 = 256 bytes = 32 threads * 16 bytes = 4 warps
        //

... (7022 more chars)

import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math
import triton
import triton.language as tl

# Build a wrapper that does the full forward with the v2 kernel
# Try different (pps, num_warps) combos
def time_kernel(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, nw, ns_actual, n_warmup=3, n_iter=15):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    num_splits = ns_actual
    q = torch.randn(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda') * 0.1
    kvc = torch.randn(1024, P, Hkv, 2*D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda') * 0.1
    bt = torch.zeros(B, num_pages, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
    sl = torch.full((B,), L, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
    out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    grid_split = (B, Hkv, num_splits)
    scale = 1.0 / math.sqrt(D)
    
    def run():
        solution._paged_decode_split_kernel[grid_split](
            q, kvc, bt, sl, mp, lp, ap,
            q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
            kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
            bt.stride(0),
            mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
            lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
            ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
            SCALE=scale,
            G=G, D=D, P=P, PAGES_PER_SPLIT=pps,
            num_warps=nw,
        )
        solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[(B, Hkv)](
            mp, lp, ap, out,
            mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
            lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
            ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
            out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
            G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=num_splits,
        )
    for _ in range(n_warmup):
        run()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        run()
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

            except Exception as e:
                pass
    print(f'  best: pps={best[1]} nw={best[2]} t={best[0]*1000:.0f}us')
    best_per_shape[sh[0]] = best

"""Sweep by directly calling the bench code"""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math
import statistics
import time

_L2_FLUSH_BYTES = 128 * 1024 * 1024
_l2_scratch = None

def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(_L2_FLUSH_BYTES // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()

def time_fn(fn, inputs, iters=20, warmup=5):
    for _ in range(warmup):
        with torch.no_grad():
            fn(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(iters):
        _l2_flush()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        with torch.no_grad():
            fn(*inputs)
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    return statistics.median(times)

def time_with(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, nw, num_splits, n_warmup=3, n_iter=15):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    
    class PatchedModel(solution.Model):
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw):
            super().__init__(*a, **kw)
            self.pages_per_split = pps
            self.num_splits = num_splits
            self._nw = nw
        
        def forward(self, q, kvc, bt, sl):
            import math as m
            B, H, D = q.shape
            Hkv = self.num_kv_heads
            G = H // Hkv
            P = self.page_size
            scale = 1.0 / m.sqrt(D)
            mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=q.dtype, device=q.device)
            grid_split = (B, Hkv, self.num_splits)
            solution._paged_decode_split_kernel[grid_split](
                q, kvc, bt, sl, mp, lp, ap,
                q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
                kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
                bt.stride(0),
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                SCALE=scale,
                G=G, D=D, P=P, PAGES_PER_SPLIT=self.pages_per_split,
                num_warps=self._nw,
            )
            grid_reduce = (B, Hkv)
            solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[grid_reduce](
                mp, lp, ap, out,
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
                G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=self.num_splits,
            )
            return out
    
    sol = PatchedModel(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    return time_fn(sol, inputs, iters=n_iter, warmup=n_warmup)

"""CUDA C++ kernel for paged attention decode (load_inline)."""
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import math
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

CUDA_SRC = r"""
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <cuda_fp16.h>
#include <torch/extension.h>

// Vector type: 4 bf16 = 8 bytes
typedef struct __align__(8)  { __nv_bfloat16 x[4]; } bf16x4_t;
// 8 bf16 = 16 bytes
typedef struct __align__(16) { __nv_bfloat16 x[8]; } bf16x8_t;

template <int G, int D, int P, int PAGES_PER_SPLIT, int THREADS>
__global__ __launch_bounds__(THREADS) void paged_decode_split(
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Q,        // (B, H, D)
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ KV,       // (num_blocks, P, Hkv, 2D)
    const int* __restrict__ BT,                 // (B, max_pages)
    const int* __restrict__ SL,                 // (B,)
    float* __restrict__ M_partial,               // (B, Hkv, NUM_SPLITS, G)
    float* __restrict__ L_partial,               // (B, Hkv, NUM_SPLITS, G)
    float* __restrict__ ACC_partial,             // (B, Hkv, NUM_SPLITS, G, D)
    int stride_qb, int stride_qh,
    int stride_kvp, int stride_kvt, int stride_kvh,
    int stride_btb,
    int stride_mb, int stride_mh, int stride_ms,
    int stride_lb, int stride_lh, int stride_ls,
    int stride_accb, int stride_acch, int stride_accs,
    float scale
) {
    int pid_b = blockIdx.x;
    int pid_hkv = blockIdx.y;
    int pid_split = blockIdx.z;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;

    int seq_len = SL[pid_b];
    int num_pages = (seq_len + P - 1) / P;
    int page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT;
    int page_end = min(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages);

    // Shared memory
    extern __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem[];
    __nv_bfloat16* q_smem = smem;                  // (G, D)
    __nv_bfloat16* k_smem = q_smem + G * D;        // (P, D)
    __nv_bfloat16* v_smem = k_smem + P * D;        // (P, D)
    float* acc_smem = (float*)(v_smem + P * D);    // (G, D)
    float* m_smem = acc_smem + G * D;              // (G,)
    float* l_smem = m_smem + G;                    // (G,)
    float* scores_smem = l_smem + G;               // (G, P)

    // Load Q
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) {
        int g = i / D;
        int d = i % D;
        int q_off = pid_b * stride_qb + (pid_hkv * G + g) * stride_qh + d;
        q_smem[i] = Q[q_off];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Init acc, m, l
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) acc_smem[i] = 0.0f;
    if (tid < G) { m_smem[tid] = -INFINITY; l_smem[tid] = 0.0f; }
    __syncthreads();

    // Per-iteration buffers
    constexpr int K_VEC = D / 8;  // 16 for D=128, 8 for D=64
    constexpr int K_VEC_TOTAL = P * K_VEC;  // P * (D/8) = 16 * 16 = 256 for D=128

    for (int p_idx = page_start; p_idx < page_end; p_idx++) {
        int page_id = BT[pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx];

        // Vectorized load of K and V (8 bf16 = 16 bytes per thread)
        // For P=16, D=128, K_VEC=16, K_VEC_TOTAL=256
        // 256 vectors / 128 threads = 2 vectors per thread
        #pragma unroll
        for (int v = tid; v < K_VEC_TOTAL; v += THREADS) {
            int row = v / K_VEC;
            int col = v % K_VEC;
            int p = row;
            int d = col * 8;
            int kv_off_k = page_id * stride_kvp + p * stride_kvt + pid_hkv * stride_kvh + d;
            int kv_off_v = kv_off_k + D;
            // Load 8 bf16 = 16 bytes
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&k_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_k);
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&v_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_v);
        }
        __syncthreads();

        int page_token_start = p_idx * P;

        // Compute scores: Q @ K^T = (G, P)
        // Each thread computes some elements
        // 4 warps = 128 threads. G*P = 4*16 = 64 elements. 1 thread per (g, p) with 64 threads.
        // We have 128 threads, so half

#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_bf16.h>

typedef struct __align__(8)  { __nv_bfloat16 x[4]; } bf16x4_t;
typedef struct __align__(16) { __nv_bfloat16 x[8]; } bf16x8_t;

__device__ __forceinline__ float bf2f(__nv_bfloat16 v) {
    return __bfloat162float(v);
}

template <int G, int D, int P, int PAGES_PER_SPLIT, int THREADS>
__global__ __launch_bounds__(THREADS) void paged_decode_split(
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Q,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ KV,
    const int* __restrict__ BT,
    const int* __restrict__ SL,
    float* __restrict__ M_partial,
    float* __restrict__ L_partial,
    float* __restrict__ ACC_partial,
    int stride_qb, int stride_qh,
    int stride_kvp, int stride_kvt, int stride_kvh,
    int stride_btb,
    int stride_mb, int stride_mh, int stride_ms,
    int stride_lb, int stride_lh, int stride_ls,
    int stride_accb, int stride_acch, int stride_accs,
    float scale
) {
    int pid_b = blockIdx.x;
    int pid_hkv = blockIdx.y;
    int pid_split = blockIdx.z;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;

    int seq_len = SL[pid_b];
    int num_pages = (seq_len + P - 1) / P;
    int page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT;
    int page_end = min(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages);

    extern __shared__ char smem_raw[];
    __nv_bfloat16* q_smem = (__nv_bfloat16*)smem_raw;
    __nv_bfloat16* k_smem = q_smem + G * D;
    __nv_bfloat16* v_smem = k_smem + P * D;
    float* acc_smem = (float*)(v_smem + P * D);
    float* m_smem = acc_smem + G * D;
    float* l_smem = m_smem + G;
    float* scores_smem = l_smem + G;
    float* alpha_smem = scores_smem + G * P;  // (G,)

    // Load Q
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) {
        int g = i / D;
        int d = i % D;
        int q_off = pid_b * stride_qb + (pid_hkv * G + g) * stride_qh + d;
        q_smem[i] = Q[q_off];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Init acc, m, l
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) acc_smem[i] = 0.0f;
    if (tid < G) { m_smem[tid] = -INFINITY; l_smem[tid] = 0.0f; }
    __syncthreads();

    constexpr int K_VEC = D / 8;
    constexpr int K_VEC_TOTAL = P * K_VEC;

    for (int p_idx = page_start; p_idx < page_end; p_idx++) {
        int page_id = BT[pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx];

        // Vectorized load of K and V (8 bf16 = 16 bytes per thread)
        #pragma unroll
        for (int v = tid; v < K_VEC_TOTAL; v += THREADS) {
            int row = v / K_VEC;
            int col = v % K_VEC;
            int p = row;
            int d = col * 8;
            int kv_off_k = page_id * stride_kvp + p * stride_kvt + pid_hkv * stride_kvh + d;
            int kv_off_v = kv_off_k + D;
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&k_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_k);
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&v_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_v);
        }
        __syncthreads();

        int page_token_start = p_idx * P;

        // Compute scores: Q @ K^T = (G, P)
        if (tid < G * P) {
            int g = tid / P;
            int p = tid % P;
            float s = 0.0f;
            #pragma unroll
            for (int d = 0; d < D; d++) {
                s += bf2f(q_smem[g * D + d]) * bf2f(k_smem[p * D + d]);
            }
            int token_pos = page_token_start + p;
            if (token_pos >= seq_len) s = -INFINITY;
            scores_smem[tid] = s * scale;
        }
        __syncthreads();

        // Online softmax update (one thread per g)
        if (tid < G) {
            int g = tid;
            float max_s = -INFINITY;
            #pragma unroll
            for (int p = 0; p < P; p++) {
                max_s = fmaxf(max_s, scores_smem[g * P + p]);
            }
            float m_old = m_smem[g];
            float m_new = fmaxf(m_old, max_s);
            float alpha = expf(m_old - m_new);
            float l_

// Pure CUDA kernel - no torch headers
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <stdint.h>

typedef struct __align__(8)  { __nv_bfloat16 x[4]; } bf16x4_t;
typedef struct __align__(16) { __nv_bfloat16 x[8]; } bf16x8_t;

__device__ __forceinline__ float bf2f(__nv_bfloat16 v) {
    return __bfloat162float(v);
}

template <int G, int D, int P, int PAGES_PER_SPLIT, int THREADS>
__global__ __launch_bounds__(THREADS) void paged_decode_split(
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Q,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ KV,
    const int* __restrict__ BT,
    const int* __restrict__ SL,
    float* __restrict__ M_partial,
    float* __restrict__ L_partial,
    float* __restrict__ ACC_partial,
    int stride_qb, int stride_qh,
    int stride_kvp, int stride_kvt, int stride_kvh,
    int stride_btb,
    int stride_mb, int stride_mh, int stride_ms,
    int stride_lb, int stride_lh, int stride_ls,
    int stride_accb, int stride_acch, int stride_accs,
    float scale
) {
    int pid_b = blockIdx.x;
    int pid_hkv = blockIdx.y;
    int pid_split = blockIdx.z;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;

    int seq_len = SL[pid_b];
    int num_pages = (seq_len + P - 1) / P;
    int page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT;
    int page_end = min(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages);

    extern __shared__ char smem_raw[];
    __nv_bfloat16* q_smem = (__nv_bfloat16*)smem_raw;
    __nv_bfloat16* k_smem = q_smem + G * D;
    __nv_bfloat16* v_smem = k_smem + P * D;
    float* acc_smem = (float*)(v_smem + P * D);
    float* m_smem = acc_smem + G * D;
    float* l_smem = m_smem + G;
    float* scores_smem = l_smem + G;
    float* alpha_smem = scores_smem + G * P;

    // Load Q
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) {
        int g = i / D;
        int d = i % D;
        int q_off = pid_b * stride_qb + (pid_hkv * G + g) * stride_qh + d;
        q_smem[i] = Q[q_off];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Init acc, m, l
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) acc_smem[i] = 0.0f;
    if (tid < G) { m_smem[tid] = -INFINITY; l_smem[tid] = 0.0f; }
    __syncthreads();

    constexpr int K_VEC_TOTAL = P * K_VEC;

        #pragma unroll
        for (int v = tid; v < K_VEC_TOTAL; v += THREADS) {
            int row = v / K_VEC;
            int col = v % K_VEC;
            int p = row;
            int d = col * 8;
            int kv_off_k = page_id * stride_kvp + p * stride_kvt + pid_hkv * stride_kvh + d;
            int kv_off_v = kv_off_k + D;
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&k_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_k);
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&v_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_v);
        }
        __syncthreads();

        // Compute scores: Q @ K^T
        if (tid < G * P) {
            int g = tid / P;
            int p = tid % P;
            float s = 0.0f;
            #pragma unroll

            int token_pos = page_token_start + p;
            if (token_pos >= seq_len) s = -INFINITY;
            scores_smem[tid] = s * scale;

import torch
import ctypes
import sys
import math
import statistics
import time
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import reference
import solution

lib = ctypes.CDLL('/tmp/cuda_paged_build/paged_decode.so')
lib.launch_paged_decode_split.argtypes = [
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p,
    ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_void_p,
]
lib.launch_paged_decode_split.restype = None

def cuda_paged_decode(q, kvc, bt, sl, pps, num_splits, G, D, P):
    B = q.shape[0]
    H = q.shape[1]
    Hkv = kvc.shape[2] // 2 * 2  # Hkv = kvc.shape[2] / 2? no, kvc is (num_blocks, P, Hkv, 2D)
    Hkv = kvc.shape[2]
    mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    stream_ptr = torch.cuda.current_stream().cuda_stream
    lib.launch_paged_decode_split(
        B, H, Hkv, D, P, num_splits, pps, G,
        q.data_ptr(), kvc.data_ptr(), bt.data_ptr(), sl.data_ptr(),
        mp.data_ptr(), lp.data_ptr(), ap.data_ptr(),
        q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
        kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
        bt.stride(0),
        mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
        lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
        ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
        stream_ptr,
    )
    # Reduce
    solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[(B, Hkv)](
        mp, lp, ap, out,
        mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
        lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
        ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=num_splits,
    )
    return out

# Test shape 0
B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = 8, 32, 8, 128, 1024, 16
reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
torch.manual_seed(42)
q, kvc, bt, sl = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
G = H // Hkv
num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
pps = 8
num_splits = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps

cuda_out = cuda_paged_decode(q, kvc, bt, sl, pps, num_splits, G, D, P)
ref = reference.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
ref_out = ref(q, kvc, bt, sl)
diff = (cuda_out.float() - ref_out.float()).abs()
print('Max abs diff:', diff.max().item())
print('Mean abs diff:', diff.mean().item())
print('All close (0.02):', torch.allclose(cuda_out.float(), ref_out.float(), atol=0.02, rtol=0.02))

import reference
import solution

lib = ctypes.CDLL('/tmp/cuda_paged_build/paged_decode.so')
lib.launch_paged_decode_split.argtypes = [
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p,

    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_void_p,
]
lib.launch_paged_decode_split.restype = None

def cuda_paged_decode(q, kvc, bt, sl, pps, num_splits, G, D, P):
    B = q.shape[0]
    H = q.shape[1]
    Hkv = kvc.shape[2]
    mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    stream_ptr = torch.cuda.current_stream().cuda_stream
    lib.launch_paged_decode_split(
        B, H, Hkv, D, P, num_splits, pps, G,
        q.data_ptr(), kvc.data_ptr(), bt.data_ptr(), sl.data_ptr(),
        mp.data_ptr(), lp.data_ptr(), ap.data_ptr(),
        q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
        kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
        bt.stride(0),
        mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
        lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
        ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
        stream_ptr,
    )
    solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[(B, Hkv)](
        mp, lp, ap, out,
        mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
        lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
        ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=num_splits,
    )
    return out

_l2_scratch = None
def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(128 * 1024 * 1024 // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()

shapes = [
    ('shape0', 8, 32, 8, 128, 1024, 16),
    ('shape1', 32, 32, 8, 128, 2048, 16),
    ('shape2', 4, 64, 8, 128, 4096, 16),
    ('shape3', 16, 32, 8, 128, 1535, 16),
    ('shape4', 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16),
]

for sh in shapes:
    B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
    print(f'=== {sh[0]} B={B} H={H} Hkv={Hkv} D={D} L={L} ===')
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    
    for pps in [4, 8, 16, 32, 64]:
        num_splits = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps
        def run():
            cuda_paged_decode(*inputs, pps, num_splits, G, D, P)
        try:
            for _ in range(3):
                run()
            torch.cuda.synchronize()
            times = []
            for _ in range(20):
                _l2_flush()
                torch.cuda.synchronize()
                s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
                e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
                s.record()
                run()
                e.record()
                torch.cuda.synchronize()
                times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
            times.sort()
            median = times[len(times)//2]
            bytes_moved = 2 * B * L * Hkv * D * 2 + B * H * D * 2 * 2
            gbps = bytes_moved / median / 10

The CUDA kernel is suboptimal. Let me think why. For CUDA, the loop is unrolled and the accesses are explicit. The Triton kernel has auto-optimization. Possible issues with my CUDA kernel: 1. The bottleneck is memory. Let me think about the memory access more carefully. For the CUDA kernel: - K load: 32 threads load 32 cache lines via 32 LDG.128. This is fully coalesced if the cache lines are contiguous. - For one (page, t, hkv), K is 128 bf16 (for D=128) = 256 bytes = 2 cache lines. With 32 threads, 32 * 16 bytes = 512 bytes. For 16 rows per page, 16 cache line accesses per K. 8 warps per row * 16 rows = 128 cache line accesses per K load (with 8 warps in the block). Wait, 4 warps per block * 32 threads = 128 threads. For one K row of 256 bytes (2 cache lines), 16 threads can cover it (16 * 16 = 256). So 16 threads do 1 LDG.128 each. The other 112 threads are idle. Or 32 threads do 1 LDG.64 each. The other 96 are idle. In my CUDA kernel, the load is: ```cuda for (int v = tid; v < K_VEC_TOTAL; v += THREADS) { int row = v / K_VEC; int col = v % K_VEC; int p = row; int d = col * 8; int kv_off_k = page_id * stride_kvp + p * stride_kvt + pid_hkv * stride_kvh + d; *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&k_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_k); } ``` K_VEC = D/8 = 16 (for D=128). K_VEC_TOTAL = P * K_VEC = 16 * 16 = 256. Each iteration loads 8 bf16 (16 bytes) into shared memory. With 128 threads, 256/128 = 2 iterations per thread. For one (p, d) chunk: 8 bf16 = 16 bytes. With 32 threads in a warp, 32 * 16 = 512 bytes. We only want 128 bytes (1 row of D=128). So 8 threads (out of 32) do 1 LDG.128 each. 24 threads idle. Or 32 threads do partial loads. Hmm, the threads in a warp cover (p, d) chunks, but the chunks are 16 bytes each. With 32 threads in a warp, the warp covers 32 chunks. For K_VEC=16 chunks per row, 2 rows per warp. So 16 chunks (1 row) + 16 chunks (next row) per warp. For (p=0, d=0..112) and (p=1, d=0..112): 32 threads load 32 chunks of 16 bytes = 512 bytes. We only have 256 bytes (2 cache lines) for these 2 rows. So 16 threads idle, 16 threads do 1 LDG.128 each. So 50% efficiency for the load. Not great. Let me restructure: have each thread load 2 bytes (1 bf16) or 4 bytes (2 bf16). Or 16 bytes (8 bf16) but in a more efficient pattern. Actually, the issue is that with 32 threads per warp and 16 bytes per thread (LDG.128), the warp covers 512 bytes. For our 256-byte row, half the warp is wasted. If I use LDG.64 (8 bytes per thread), the warp covers 256 bytes = 1 row. So 1 LDG.64 per thread = 1 instruction per warp per row. 16 rows = 16 instructions per warp per K load. """Find the best per-shape pps and write a heuristic."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math
import statistics

_l2_scratch = None
def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(128 * 1024 * 1024 // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()


def time_shape(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, n_warmup=3, n_iter=15):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    num_splits = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps
    
    class PatchedModel(solution.Model):
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw):
            super().__init__(*a, **kw)
            self.pages_per_split = pps
            self.num_splits = num_splits
    
    sol = PatchedModel(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    for _ in range(n_warmup):
        sol(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        _l2_flush()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        sol(*inputs)
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]


shapes = [
    ('shape0', 8, 32, 8, 128, 1024, 16),
    ('shape1', 32, 32, 8, 128, 2048, 16),
    ('shape2', 4, 64, 8, 128, 4096, 16),
    ('shape3', 16, 32, 8, 128, 1535, 16),
    ('shape4', 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16),
]

best = {}
for sh in shapes:
    B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    best_t = float('inf')
    best_pps = None
    for pps in [4, 8, 16, 32, 64, 128]:
        if pps > num_pages and pps != 128:
            continue
        try:
            t = time_shape(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps)
            if t < best_t:
                best_t = t
                best_pps = pps
        except Exception as e:
            pass
    best[sh[0]] = (best_pps, best_t)
    print(f'{sh[0]}: best pps={best_pps} t={best_t*1000:.0f}us')

# Compute geomean
import math
log_sum = 0
count = 0
for sh in shapes:
    B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
    t = best[sh[0]][1]
    bytes_moved = 2 * B * L * Hkv * D * 2 + B * H * D * 2 * 2
    gbps = bytes_moved / (t * 1e-3) / 1e9
    frac = gbps / 936
    log_sum += math.log(max(frac, 1e-9))
    count += 1
gmean = math.exp(log_sum / count)
print(f'GMEAN (per-shape best) = {gmean:.4f}')

# Compute with current heuristic
def heuristic_pps(B, Hkv, L, P):
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    workload = B * Hkv * num_pages
    if workload < 8192:
        return 8
    elif workload < 16384:
        return 32
    else:
        return 64
    return min(pps, num_pages)

log_sum = 0
for sh in shapes:
    B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
    pps = heuristic_pps(B, Hkv, L, P)
    t = time_shape(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps)
    bytes_moved = 2 * B * L * Hkv * D * 2 + B * H * D * 2 * 2
    gbps = bytes_moved / (t * 1e-3) / 1e9
    frac = gbps / 936
    log_sum += math.log(max(frac, 1e-9))
gmean_h = math.exp(log_sum / count)
print(f'GMEAN (current heuristic) = {gmean_h:.4f}')

"""Try a 2-pages-per-iter variant."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math
import triton
import triton.language as tl

# Modified kernel: process 2 pages per iteration
@triton.jit
def _paged_decode_split_kernel_2p(
    Q_ptr, KV_ptr, BT_ptr, SL_ptr,
    M_ptr, L_ptr, ACC_ptr,
    stride_qb, stride_qh,
    stride_kvp, stride_kvt, stride_kvh,
    stride_btb,
    stride_mb, stride_mh, stride_ms,
    stride_lb, stride_lh, stride_ls,
    stride_accb, stride_acch, stride_accs,
    SCALE: tl.constexpr,
    G: tl.constexpr,
    D: tl.constexpr,
    P: tl.constexpr,           # page_size
    PAGES_PER_SPLIT: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_b = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_hkv = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_split = tl.program_id(2)

    seq_len = tl.load(SL_ptr + pid_b)
    num_pages = tl.cdiv(seq_len, P)

    page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT
    page_end = tl.minimum(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages)

    head_offs = pid_hkv * G + tl.arange(0, G)
    d_offs = tl.arange(0, D)
    q_ptrs = (Q_ptr + pid_b * stride_qb
              + head_offs[:, None] * stride_qh
              + d_offs[None, :])
    q = tl.load(q_ptrs)

    m_i = tl.full((G,), -float('inf'), dtype=tl.float32)
    l_i = tl.zeros((G,), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc = tl.zeros((G, D), dtype=tl.float32)

    # Process 2 pages per iteration
    P2: tl.constexpr = 2 * P
    t_offs_2p = tl.arange(0, P2)
    
    p_idx = page_start
    while p_idx + 1 < page_end:
        # Load 2 page_ids
        page_id_0 = tl.load(BT_ptr + pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx).to(tl.int64)
        page_id_1 = tl.load(BT_ptr + pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx + 1).to(tl.int64)
        
        # Compute masks
        page_token_start = p_idx * P
        token_mask = (page_token_start + t_offs_2p) < seq_len  # (2P,)
        
        # Load K and V for 2 pages: (2P, D)
        # K for first page at p_idx, K for second at p_idx+1
        # We need to gather them since they're at different page_ids
        # For simplicity, load 2 separate (P, D) tiles
        
        # K page 0
        base0 = (KV_ptr + page_id_0 * stride_kvp
                 + tl.arange(0, P)[:, None] * stride_kvt
                 + pid_hkv * stride_kvh)
        t_offs = tl.arange(0, P)
        k0 = tl.load(base0 + d_offs[None, :])  # (P, D)
        v0 = tl.load(base0 + (D + d_offs[None, :]))
        
        # K page 1
        base1 = (KV_ptr + page_id_1 * stride_kvp
                 + t_offs[:, None] * stride_kvt
                 + pid_hkv * stride_kvh)
        k1 = tl.load(base1 + d_offs[None, :])
        v1 = tl.load(base1 + (D + d_offs[None, :]))
        
        # Concatenate K and V along P dim
        # (2P, D) by stacking
        k = tl.cat(k0, k1, can_reorder=True)  # might not be supported
        v = tl.cat(v0, v1, can_reorder=True)
        
        # Mask
        token_mask0 = (page_token_start + t_offs) < seq_len
        token_mask1 = (page_token_start + P + t_offs) < seq_len
        
        # Compute scores
        scores = tl.dot(q, tl.trans(k)) * SCALE
        scores = tl.where(tl.cat(token_mask0[None, :], token_mask1[None, :], can_reorder=True), scores, -float('inf'))
        
        # Online softmax
        m_new = tl.maximum(m_i, tl.max(scores, axis=1))
        alpha = tl.exp(m_i - m_new)
        p_block = tl.exp(scores - m_new[:, None])
        l_i = l_i * alpha + tl.sum(p_block, axis=1)
        acc = acc * alpha[:, None] + tl.dot(p_block.to(v.dtype), v)
        m_i = m_new
        
        p_idx += 2
    
    # Handle remaining single page
    if p_idx < page_end:
        page_id = tl.load(BT_ptr + pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx).to(tl.int64)
        page_token_start = p_idx * P
        token_mask = (page_token_start + t

import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math

_l2_scratch = None
def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(128 * 1024 * 1024 // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()

def time_with_nw(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, nw, num_splits, n_warmup=3, n_iter=15):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    
    class PatchedModel(solution.Model):
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw):
            super().__init__(*a, **kw)
            self.pages_per_split = pps
            self.num_splits = num_splits
            self._nw = nw
        def forward(self, q, kvc, bt, sl):
            import math as m
            B, H, D = q.shape
            Hkv = self.num_kv_heads
            G = H // Hkv
            P = self.page_size
            scale = 1.0 / m.sqrt(D)
            mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=q.dtype, device=q.device)
            grid_split = (B, Hkv, self.num_splits)
            solution._paged_decode_split_kernel[grid_split](
                q, kvc, bt, sl, mp, lp, ap,
                q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
                kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
                bt.stride(0),
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                SCALE=scale,
                G=G, D=D, P=P, PAGES_PER_SPLIT=self.pages_per_split,
                num_warps=self._nw,
            )
            solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[(B, Hkv)](
                mp, lp, ap, out,
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
                G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=self.num_splits,
            )
            return out
    
    sol = PatchedModel(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    for _ in range(n_warmup):
        sol(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        _l2_flush()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        sol(*inputs)
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

shapes = [
    ('shape0', 8, 32, 8, 128, 1024, 16),
    ('shape1', 32, 32, 8, 128, 2048, 16),
    ('shape2', 4, 64, 8, 128, 4096, 16),
    ('shape3', 16, 32, 8, 128, 1535, 16),
    ('shape4', 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16),
]

# Sweep num_warps for each shape
for sh in shapes:
    B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = sh[1:]
    num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P
    # Find best pps
    best_pps = None
    for pps in [8, 16, 32, 64]:
        if pps > num_pages: continue
        ns = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps
        t = time_with_nw(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, 4, ns)  # default nw=4
        if best_pps is None or t < best_pps[1]:
            best_pps = (pps, t)
    best_pps, _ = best_pps
    ns = (num_pages + best_pps - 1) // best_pps

"""Paged attention decode kernel (Triton) for SM86 (RTX 3090).

Two-stage FlashDecoding approach for high SM utilization on small batches:
  Stage 1 (split): each (batch, kv_head, split) program processes a chunk of
                   pages for that kv_head and writes partial (m, l, acc).
  Stage 2 (reduce): combine splits per (batch, kv_head) into the final output.

Memory-bound; the workload is dominated by streaming the KV cache from HBM.
"""
import math

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import triton
import triton.language as tl

# --- Shape knobs (overridden by check.py / benchmark.py from shapes.py) ----
BATCH = 8
NUM_HEADS = 32
NUM_KV_HEADS = 8
HEAD_DIM = 128
SEQ_LEN = 1024
PAGE_SIZE = 16

# Target blocks: ~4 resident per SM on a 3090 (82 SMs).
_NUM_SMS_3090 = 82
_TARGET_BLOCKS = 4 * _NUM_SMS_3090


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

"""Try different approaches for shape 4 specifically."""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import torch
import importlib
import solution
import reference
importlib.reload(solution)
importlib.reload(reference)
import math

_l2_scratch = None
def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(128 * 1024 * 1024 // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()

def time_with(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, ns, nw, n_stages, n_warmup=3, n_iter=15):
    reference.BATCH = B; reference.NUM_HEADS = H; reference.NUM_KV_HEADS = Hkv
    reference.HEAD_DIM = D; reference.SEQ_LEN = L; reference.PAGE_SIZE = P
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    G = H // Hkv
    
    class PatchedModel(solution.Model):
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw):
            super().__init__(*a, **kw)
            self.pages_per_split = pps
            self.num_splits = ns
            self._nw = nw
            self._n_stages = n_stages
        def forward(self, q, kvc, bt, sl):
            import math as m
            B, H, D = q.shape
            Hkv = self.num_kv_heads
            G = H // Hkv
            P = self.page_size
            scale = 1.0 / m.sqrt(D)
            mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, self.num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device=q.device)
            out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=q.dtype, device=q.device)
            grid_split = (B, Hkv, self.num_splits)
            # We can't easily change num_stages - it's hardcoded in the kernel
            # So just use the standard kernel
            solution._paged_decode_split_kernel[grid_split](
                q, kvc, bt, sl, mp, lp, ap,
                q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
                kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
                bt.stride(0),
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                SCALE=scale,
                G=G, D=D, P=P, PAGES_PER_SPLIT=self.pages_per_split,
                num_warps=self._nw,
            )
            solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[(B, Hkv)](
                mp, lp, ap, out,
                mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
                lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
                ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
                out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
                G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=self.num_splits,
            )
            return out
    
    sol = PatchedModel(*init_args).cuda().eval()
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    inputs = [t.cuda() for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    for _ in range(n_warmup):
        sol(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        _l2_flush()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
        s.record()
        sol(*inputs)
        e.record()
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        times.append(s.elapsed_time(e))
    times.sort()
    return times[len(times)//2]

# Shape 4
B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16
num_pages = (L + P - 1) // P  # 125

print('=== Shape 4 sweep ===')
for pps in [4, 8, 16, 32, 64]:
    ns = (num_pages + pps - 1) // pps
    for nw in [1, 2, 4, 8]:
        try:
            t = time_with(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P, pps, ns, nw, 2)
            print(f'  PPS={pps:3d} NS={ns:2d} NW={nw} t={t*1000:5.0f}us')
        except Exception as e:
            print(f'  PPS={pps:3d} NS={ns:2d} NW={nw} error: {e}')

"""CUDA kernel via load_inline for paged attention decode."""
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import math
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

CUDA_SRC = r"""
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <stdint.h>

typedef struct __align__(8)  { __nv_bfloat16 x[4]; } bf16x4_t;
typedef struct __align__(16) { __nv_bfloat16 x[8]; } bf16x8_t;

__device__ __forceinline__ float bf16_to_f32(__nv_bfloat16 v) {
    uint32_t bits = (uint32_t)*reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(&v);
    bits = bits << 16;
    return __int_as_float(bits);
}

__device__ __forceinline__ __nv_bfloat16 f32_to_bf16(float v) {
    uint32_t bits = __float_as_int(v);
    uint16_t b16 = (uint16_t)(bits >> 16);
    return *reinterpret_cast<__nv_bfloat16*>(&b16);
}

template <int G, int D, int P, int PAGES_PER_SPLIT, int THREADS>
__global__ __launch_bounds__(THREADS) void paged_decode_split(
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Q,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ KV,
    const int* __restrict__ BT,
    const int* __restrict__ SL,
    float* __restrict__ M_partial,
    float* __restrict__ L_partial,
    float* __restrict__ ACC_partial,
    int stride_qb, int stride_qh,
    int stride_kvp, int stride_kvt, int stride_kvh,
    int stride_btb,
    int stride_mb, int stride_mh, int stride_ms,
    int stride_lb, int stride_lh, int stride_ls,
    int stride_accb, int stride_acch, int stride_accs,
    float scale
) {
    int pid_b = blockIdx.x;
    int pid_hkv = blockIdx.y;
    int pid_split = blockIdx.z;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;

    int seq_len = SL[pid_b];
    int num_pages = (seq_len + P - 1) / P;
    int page_start = pid_split * PAGES_PER_SPLIT;
    int page_end = min(page_start + PAGES_PER_SPLIT, num_pages);

    extern __shared__ char smem_raw[];
    __nv_bfloat16* q_smem = (__nv_bfloat16*)smem_raw;
    __nv_bfloat16* k_smem = q_smem + G * D;
    __nv_bfloat16* v_smem = k_smem + P * D;
    float* acc_smem = (float*)(v_smem + P * D);
    float* m_smem = acc_smem + G * D;
    float* l_smem = m_smem + G;
    float* scores_smem = l_smem + G;
    float* alpha_smem = scores_smem + G * P;

    // Load Q
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) {
        int g = i / D;
        int d = i % D;
        int q_off = pid_b * stride_qb + (pid_hkv * G + g) * stride_qh + d;
        q_smem[i] = Q[q_off];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Init acc, m, l
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = tid; i < G * D; i += THREADS) acc_smem[i] = 0.0f;
    if (tid < G) { m_smem[tid] = -INFINITY; l_smem[tid] = 0.0f; }
    __syncthreads();

    constexpr int K_VEC = D / 8;
    constexpr int K_VEC_TOTAL = P * K_VEC;

    for (int p_idx = page_start; p_idx < page_end; p_idx++) {
        int page_id = BT[pid_b * stride_btb + p_idx];

        // Vectorized load of K and V
        #pragma unroll
        for (int v = tid; v < K_VEC_TOTAL; v += THREADS) {
            int row = v / K_VEC;
            int col = v % K_VEC;
            int p = row;
            int d = col * 8;
            int kv_off_k = page_id * stride_kvp + p * stride_kvt + pid_hkv * stride_kvh + d;
            int kv_off_v = kv_off_k + D;
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&k_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_k);
            *reinterpret_cast<bf16x8_t*>(&v_smem[p * D + d]) = *reinterpret_cast<const bf16x8_t*>(KV + kv_off_v);
        }
        __syncthreads();

        int page_token_start = p_idx * P;

        // Compute scores: Q @ K^T
        if (tid < G * P) {
            int g = tid / P;
            int p = tid % P;
            float s = 0.0f;
            #pragma unroll
            for (int d = 0; d < D; d++) {
                s += bf16_to_f32(q_smem[g * D + d]) * bf16_to_f32(k_smem[p * D + d]);
            }
            int token_pos = page_token_start + p;
            if (token_pos >= seq_len) s = -INFINITY;
            scores_smem[tid] = s * scale;
        }
        __syncthreads();

        // Online softmax
        if (tid < G)

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import math
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

CUDA_SRC = r"""
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <stdint.h>

typedef struct __align__(8)  { __nv_bfloat16 x[4]; } bf16x4_t;
typedef struct __align__(16) { __nv_bfloat16 x[8]; } bf16x8_t;

__device__ __forceinline__ float bf16_to_f32(__nv_bfloat16 v) {
    unsigned short s = __bfloat16_as_ushort(v);
    unsigned int bits = ((unsigned int)s) << 16;
    return __int_as_float((int)bits);
}

template <int G, int D, int P, int PAGES_PER_SPLIT, int THREADS>
__global__ __launch_bounds__(THREADS) void paged_decode_split(
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Q,

    float* l_smem = m_smem + G;

    float* alpha_smem = scores_smem + G * P;

        }
        __syncthreads();

                scores_smem[g * P + p] = expf(scores_smem[g * P + p]

"""Test loading the CUDA .so file and using it."""
import torch
import ctypes
import math
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260618_183353_minimax-claude_MiniMax-M3_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention')
import reference
import solution

# Load the .so file
lib = ctypes.CDLL('/tmp/cuda_paged_build/paged_decode.so')
lib.launch_paged_decode_split.argtypes = [
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p,
    ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p, ctypes.c_void_p,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int, ctypes.c_int,
    ctypes.c_void_p,
]
lib.launch_paged_decode_split.restype = None

_l2_scratch = None
def _l2_flush():
    global _l2_scratch
    if _l2_scratch is None:
        _l2_scratch = torch.empty(128 * 1024 * 1024 // 4, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    _l2_scratch.zero_()

def cuda_decode(q, kvc, bt, sl, pps, num_splits, G, D, P):
    B = q.shape[0]
    H = q.shape[1]
    Hkv = kvc.shape[2]
    mp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    lp = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    ap = torch.empty(B, Hkv, num_splits, G, D, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    stream_ptr = torch.cuda.current_stream().cuda_stream
    lib.launch_paged_decode_split(
        B, H, Hkv, D, P, num_splits, pps, G,
        q.data_ptr(), kvc.data_ptr(), bt.data_ptr(), sl.data_ptr(),
        mp.data_ptr(), lp.data_ptr(), ap.data_ptr(),
        q.stride(0), q.stride(1),
        kvc.stride(0), kvc.stride(1), kvc.stride(2),
        bt.stride(0),
        mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
        lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
        ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
        stream_ptr,
    )
    solution._paged_decode_reduce_kernel[(B, Hkv)](
        mp, lp, ap, out,
        mp.stride(0), mp.stride(1), mp.stride(2),
        lp.stride(0), lp.stride(1), lp.stride(2),
        ap.stride(0), ap.stride(1), ap.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        G=G, D=D, NUM_SPLITS=num_splits,
    )
    return out

shapes = [
    ('shape0', 8, 32, 8, 128, 1024, 16),
    ('shape1', 32, 32, 8, 128, 2048, 16),
    ('shape2', 4, 64, 8, 128, 4096, 16),
    ('shape3', 16, 32, 8, 128, 1535, 16),
    ('shape4', 8, 16, 4, 64, 2000, 16),
]

# Per-shape best PPS for CUDA
best_pps = {

for sh in shapes:
